<a id="612" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="619" href="FrameOfNuclei.html" class="Module">FrameOfNuclei</a> <a id="633" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="634" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="636" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="638" href="Frame.html#3701" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="644" href="Basis.html#2446" class="Generalizable">ℓ₀</a> <a id="647" href="Basis.html#2449" class="Generalizable">ℓ₁</a> <a id="650" href="Basis.html#2452" class="Generalizable">ℓ₂</a><a id="652" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="654" class="Keyword">where</a>
</pre>
**Based on work by Martín Escardó.**

Preliminaries
=============

We assume a fixed frame `F` on which to define the frame of nuclei.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="809" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="814" href="Poset.html#3652" class="Module">PosetReasoning</a> <a id="829" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="830" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="834" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a><a id="835" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="837" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="843" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="844" href="Poset.html#3694" class="Function Operator">_⊑⟨_⟩_</a><a id="850" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="852" href="Poset.html#3832" class="Function Operator">_■</a><a id="854" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
For simplicity, we will refer to the meet of `F` simply as `_⊓_`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊓_"></a><a id="936" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#936" class="Function Operator">_⊓_</a> <a id="940" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="942" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="944" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="946" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="949" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="951" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="953" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="955" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="958" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="960" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="962" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="964" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a>
<a id="967" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#967" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="969" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#936" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="971" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#971" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="973" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="975" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#967" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="977" href="Frame.html#4167" class="Function">⊓[</a> <a id="980" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="982" href="Frame.html#4167" class="Function">]</a> <a id="984" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#971" class="Bound">y</a>
</pre>
Poset of nuclei on `F`
======================

The set of endofunctions on a given frame forms a poset.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊑f_"></a><a id="1104" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1104" class="Function Operator">_⊑f_</a> <a id="1109" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1111" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1112" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1114" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1116" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1119" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1121" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1123" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1125" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="1127" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1129" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1131" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1132" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1134" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1136" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1139" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1141" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1143" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1145" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="1147" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1149" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1151" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#1500" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="1157" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1158" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1202" class="Primitive">ℓ-max</a> <a id="1164" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#644" class="Bound">ℓ₀</a> <a id="1167" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#647" class="Bound">ℓ₁</a><a id="1169" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="1171" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1171" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="1173" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1104" class="Function Operator">⊑f</a> <a id="1176" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1176" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="1178" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1180" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#4500" class="Function">∀[</a> <a id="1183" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1183" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1185" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#4500" class="Function">∶</a> <a id="1187" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1189" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1191" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1194" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#4500" class="Function">]</a> <a id="1196" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1171" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="1198" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1183" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1200" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="1203" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="1207" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1209" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="1211" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1176" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="1213" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1183" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="⊑f-refl"></a><a id="1216" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1216" class="Function">⊑f-refl</a> <a id="1224" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1226" href="Basis.html#1591" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="1228" href="Poset.html#469" class="Function">isReflexive</a> <a id="1240" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1104" class="Function Operator">_⊑f_</a> <a id="1245" href="Basis.html#1591" class="Function Operator">]</a>
<a id="1247" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1216" class="Function">⊑f-refl</a> <a id="1255" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1255" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="1257" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1257" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1259" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1261" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">⊑[</a> <a id="1264" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="1268" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1270" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">]-refl</a> <a id="1277" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1278" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1255" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="1280" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1257" class="Bound">x</a><a id="1281" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="⊑f-trans"></a><a id="1284" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1284" class="Function">⊑f-trans</a> <a id="1293" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1295" href="Basis.html#1591" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="1297" href="Poset.html#622" class="Function">isTransitive</a> <a id="1310" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1104" class="Function Operator">_⊑f_</a> <a id="1315" href="Basis.html#1591" class="Function Operator">]</a>
<a id="1317" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1284" class="Function">⊑f-trans</a> <a id="1326" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1326" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="1328" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1328" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="1330" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1330" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="1332" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1332" class="Bound">f⊑g</a> <a id="1336" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1336" class="Bound">g⊑h</a> <a id="1340" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1340" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1342" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1344" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1326" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="1346" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1340" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1348" href="Poset.html#3694" class="Function Operator">⊑⟨</a> <a id="1351" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1332" class="Bound">f⊑g</a> <a id="1355" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1340" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1357" href="Poset.html#3694" class="Function Operator">⟩</a> <a id="1359" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1328" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="1361" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1340" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1363" href="Poset.html#3694" class="Function Operator">⊑⟨</a> <a id="1366" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1336" class="Bound">g⊑h</a> <a id="1370" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1340" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1372" href="Poset.html#3694" class="Function Operator">⟩</a> <a id="1374" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1330" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="1376" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1340" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1378" href="Poset.html#3832" class="Function Operator">■</a>

<a id="is-set"></a><a id="1381" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1381" class="Function">is-set</a> <a id="1388" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1390" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#10203" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="1396" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1397" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1399" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1401" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1404" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1406" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1408" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1410" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="1412" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="1414" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1381" class="Function">is-set</a> <a id="1421" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1423" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#15852" class="Function">isSetΠ</a> <a id="1430" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="1432" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1432" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1434" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1436" href="Poset.html#3444" class="Function">carrier-is-set</a> <a id="1451" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1452" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="1456" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a><a id="1457" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="⊑f-antisym"></a><a id="1460" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1460" class="Function">⊑f-antisym</a> <a id="1471" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1473" href="Basis.html#1591" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="1475" href="Poset.html#965" class="Function">isAntisym</a> <a id="1485" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1381" class="Function">is-set</a> <a id="1492" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1104" class="Function Operator">_⊑f_</a> <a id="1497" href="Basis.html#1591" class="Function Operator">]</a>
<a id="1499" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1460" class="Function">⊑f-antisym</a> <a id="1510" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1510" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="1512" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1512" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="1514" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1514" class="Bound">f⊑g</a> <a id="1518" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1518" class="Bound">g⊑h</a> <a id="1522" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="1526" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#7957" class="Function">funExt</a> <a id="1533" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="1535" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1535" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1537" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1539" href="Poset.html#3283" class="Function Operator">⊑[</a> <a id="1542" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="1546" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1548" href="Poset.html#3283" class="Function Operator">]-antisym</a> <a id="1558" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1559" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1510" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="1561" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1535" class="Bound">x</a><a id="1562" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1564" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1565" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1512" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="1567" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1535" class="Bound">x</a><a id="1568" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1570" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1571" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1514" class="Bound">f⊑g</a> <a id="1575" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1535" class="Bound">x</a><a id="1576" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1578" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1579" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1518" class="Bound">g⊑h</a> <a id="1583" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1535" class="Bound">x</a><a id="1584" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="endopos"></a><a id="1587" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1587" class="Function">endopos</a> <a id="1595" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1597" href="Poset.html#2165" class="Function">Poset</a> <a id="1603" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#644" class="Bound">ℓ₀</a> <a id="1606" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1607" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1202" class="Primitive">ℓ-max</a> <a id="1613" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#644" class="Bound">ℓ₀</a> <a id="1616" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#647" class="Bound">ℓ₁</a><a id="1618" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="1620" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1587" class="Function">endopos</a> <a id="1628" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1630" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1631" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1633" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1635" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1638" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1640" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1642" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1644" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="1646" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1648" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="1650" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1104" class="Function Operator">_⊑f_</a> <a id="1655" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="1657" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1381" class="Function">is-set</a> <a id="1664" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="1666" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1216" class="Function">⊑f-refl</a> <a id="1674" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="1676" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1284" class="Function">⊑f-trans</a> <a id="1685" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="1687" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1460" class="Function">⊑f-antisym</a>
</pre>
Therefore, the poset of nuclei on a frame forms a poset.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊑N_"></a><a id="1769" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1769" class="Function Operator">_⊑N_</a> <a id="1774" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1776" href="Poset.html#275" class="Function">Order</a> <a id="1782" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1783" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1202" class="Primitive">ℓ-max</a> <a id="1789" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#644" class="Bound">ℓ₀</a> <a id="1792" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#647" class="Bound">ℓ₁</a><a id="1794" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1796" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1797" href="Nucleus.html#578" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="1805" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a><a id="1806" class="Symbol">)</a>

Frame of nuclei on `F`
======================

The top nucleus
---------------

The meet of two nuclei
----------------------

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊓N_"></a><a id="2790" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2790" class="Function Operator">_⊓N_</a> <a id="2795" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2797" href="Nucleus.html#578" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="2805" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2807" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2809" href="Nucleus.html#578" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="2817" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2819" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2821" href="Nucleus.html#578" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="2829" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a>

  <a id="2892" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="2895" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2895" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2897" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2899" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2834" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="2901" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2895" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2903" href="Frame.html#4167" class="Function">⊓[</a> <a id="2906" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2908" href="Frame.html#4167" class="Function">]</a> <a id="2910" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2864" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="2912" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2895" class="Bound">x</a><a id="2913" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2915" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2917" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2948" class="Function">⊓-N₀</a> <a id="2922" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2924" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3711" class="Function">⊓-N₁</a> <a id="2929" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2931" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3786" class="Function">⊓-N₂</a>
  <a id="2938" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="2948" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2948" class="Function">⊓-N₀</a> <a id="2953" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2955" class="Symbol">_</a>

                      <a id="4683" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4685" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="4688" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4688" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4690" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4692" href="Frame.html#5063" class="Function Operator">⊓[</a> <a id="4695" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="4697" href="Frame.html#5063" class="Function Operator">]-lower₁</a> <a id="4706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4707" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4610" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="4709" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4688" class="Bound">x</a><a id="4710" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4712" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4713" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4618" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4715" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4688" class="Bound">x</a><a id="4716" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="4722" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4722" class="Function">greatest</a> <a id="4731" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4733" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4734" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4734" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="4736" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4736" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4738" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4738" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4740" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4742" href="Nucleus.html#578" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="4750" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a><a id="4751" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4753" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4755" href="Basis.html#1591" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="4757" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4738" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4759" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1769" class="Function Operator">⊑N</a> <a id="4762" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4734" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="4764" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#606" class="Function Operator">∧</a> <a id="4766" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4738" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4768" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1769" class="Function Operator">⊑N</a> <a id="4771" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4736" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4773" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#1956" class="Function Operator">⇒</a> <a id="4775" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4738" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4777" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1769" class="Function Operator">⊑N</a> <a id="4780" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4781" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4734" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="4783" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2790" class="Function Operator">⊓N</a> <a id="4786" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4736" class="Bound">k</a><a id="4787" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4789" href="Basis.html#1591" class="Function Operator">]</a>
  <a id="4793" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4722" class="Function">greatest</a> <a id="4802" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4803" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4803" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="4805" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4807" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="4810" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4811" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4811" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4813" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4815" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="4818" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4819" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4819" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4821" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4823" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="4826" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4827" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4827" class="Bound">l⊑j</a> <a id="4831" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4833" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4833" class="Bound">l⊑k</a><a id="4836" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4838" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4838" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4840" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="4846" href="Frame.html#5193" class="Function Operator">⊓[</a> <a id="4849" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="4851" href="Frame.html#5193" class="Function Operator">]-greatest</a> <a id="4862" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4863" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4803" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="4865" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4838" class="Bound">x</a><a id="4866" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4868" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4869" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4811" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4871" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4838" class="Bound">x</a><a id="4872" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4874" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4875" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4819" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4877" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4838" class="Bound">x</a><a id="4878" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4880" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4881" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4827" class="Bound">l⊑j</a> <a id="4885" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4838" class="Bound">x</a><a id="4886" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4888" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4889" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4833" class="Bound">l⊑k</a> <a id="4893" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#4838" class="Bound">x</a><a id="4894" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>
Arbitrary join of nuclei
------------------------

This is the non-trivial part of this development.

Given a family `α` of endofunctions on a type, we denote by `compFam α` the
family obtained by taking compositions of functions in `α`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="compFam"></a><a id="5149" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5149" class="Function">compFam</a> <a id="5157" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5159" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5160" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5160" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5162" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5164" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1230" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="5169" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#644" class="Bound">ℓ₀</a><a id="5171" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5173" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5174" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5174" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="5176" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5178" href="Basis.html#4764" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="5182" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#650" class="Bound">ℓ₂</a> <a id="5185" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5186" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5160" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5188" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5190" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5160" class="Bound">A</a><a id="5191" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5194" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5196" href="Basis.html#4764" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="5200" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#650" class="Bound">ℓ₂</a> <a id="5203" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5204" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5160" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5206" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5208" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5160" class="Bound">A</a><a id="5209" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5211" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5149" class="Function">compFam</a> <a id="5219" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5220" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="5222" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5224" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5224" class="Bound">A</a><a id="5225" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5227" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5227" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="5229" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5231" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#148" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="5236" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5237" href="Basis.html#4839" class="Function">index</a> <a id="5243" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5227" class="Bound">α</a><a id="5244" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5246" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="5248" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5259" class="Function">f</a> <a id="5250" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="5259" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5259" class="Function">f</a> <a id="5261" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5263" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#148" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="5268" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5269" href="Basis.html#4839" class="Function">index</a> <a id="5275" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5227" class="Bound">α</a><a id="5276" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5278" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5280" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5224" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5282" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5284" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5224" class="Bound">A</a>
  <a id="5288" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5259" class="Function">f</a> <a id="5290" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#185" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>       <a id="5299" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5301" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#344" class="Function">idfun</a> <a id="5307" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5224" class="Bound">A</a>
  <a id="5311" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5259" class="Function">f</a> <a id="5313" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5314" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5314" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="5316" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#200" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="5318" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5318" class="Bound">is</a><a id="5320" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5322" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5324" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5259" class="Function">f</a> <a id="5326" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5318" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="5329" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="5331" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5332" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5227" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="5334" href="Basis.html#4932" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="5336" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5314" class="Bound">i</a><a id="5337" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
We will use this function to compute the join of a family of nuclei.

Notice that the identity function is always a (pre)nucleus.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="id-is-nuclear"></a><a id="5483" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5483" class="Function">id-is-nuclear</a> <a id="5497" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5499" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5500" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5500" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="5502" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5504" href="Frame.html#3701" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="5510" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#644" class="Bound">ℓ₀</a> <a id="5513" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#647" class="Bound">ℓ₁</a> <a id="5516" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#650" class="Bound">ℓ₂</a><a id="5518" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5520" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5522" href="Prenucleus.html#493" class="Function">isPrenuclear</a> <a id="5535" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5500" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="5537" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5538" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#344" class="Function">idfun</a> <a id="5544" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="5546" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5500" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="5548" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="5550" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5552" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5483" class="Function">id-is-nuclear</a> <a id="5566" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5566" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="5568" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5570" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="5573" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5573" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="5575" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5575" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="5577" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5579" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#898" class="Function">refl</a><a id="5583" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5585" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="5587" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">⊑[</a> <a id="5590" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="5594" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5566" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="5596" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">]-refl</a>
</pre>
Compositions of prenuclei are prenuclei meaning given a family of nuclei, its
`compFam` is a family of prenuclei

<pre class="Agda"><a id="compFam-prenucleus"></a><a id="5730" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5730" class="Function">compFam-prenucleus</a> <a id="5749" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5751" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5752" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5752" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="5754" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5756" href="Basis.html#4764" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="5760" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#650" class="Bound">ℓ₂</a> <a id="5763" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5764" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="5766" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="5768" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="5771" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5773" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="5775" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="5777" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="5779" class="Symbol">))</a>

</pre>
For convenience, we introduce the following notation: given a some family
`J` of nuclei, `J ^*` denotes its `compFam`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_^*"></a><a id="6882" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6882" class="Function Operator">_^*</a> <a id="6886" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6888" href="Basis.html#4764" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="6892" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#650" class="Bound">ℓ₂</a> <a id="6895" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6896" href="Nucleus.html#578" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="6904" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a><a id="6905" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6907" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6909" href="Basis.html#4764" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="6913" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#650" class="Bound">ℓ₂</a> <a id="6916" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6917" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="6919" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6921" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="6924" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6926" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="6928" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6930" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="6932" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="6934" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6934" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="6936" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6882" class="Function Operator">^*</a> <a id="6939" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6941" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5149" class="Function">compFam</a> <a id="6949" href="Basis.html#5346" class="Function">⁅</a> <a id="6951" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6956" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6953" href="Basis.html#5346" class="Function">∣</a> <a id="6955" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6955" class="Bound">(</a><a id="6956" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6956" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6958" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6960" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6955" class="Bound">_)</a> <a id="6963" href="Basis.html#5346" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="6965" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6934" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="6967" href="Basis.html#5346" class="Function">⁆</a>

      <a id="7280" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7282" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7283" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7283" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="7286" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7286" class="Bound">js</a> <a id="7289" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7291" href="Basis.html#4839" class="Function">index</a> <a id="7297" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7298" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7250" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="7300" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6882" class="Function Operator">^*</a><a id="7302" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="7305" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7307" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7250" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="7309" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6882" class="Function Operator">^*</a> <a id="7312" href="Basis.html#4932" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="7314" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7315" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7283" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="7318" href="Cubical.Data.List.Base.html#335" class="Function Operator">++</a> <a id="7321" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7286" class="Bound">js</a><a id="7323" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7325" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="7327" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7328" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7250" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="7330" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6882" class="Function Operator">^*</a> <a id="7333" href="Basis.html#4932" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="7335" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7286" class="Bound">js</a><a id="7337" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7339" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="7341" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7342" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7250" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="7344" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6882" class="Function Operator">^*</a> <a id="7347" href="Basis.html#4932" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="7349" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7283" class="Bound">is</a><a id="7351" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>
`J ^*` is always inhabited.

</pre>
Some nice notation.

<a id="9209" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9131" class="Function">isScottContinuous</a> <a id="9227" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9227" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="9229" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="9233" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9234" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9234" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="9236" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9238" href="Basis.html#4764" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="9242" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#650" class="Bound">ℓ₂</a> <a id="9245" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="9247" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9249" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="9251" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9253" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="9259" href="Basis.html#1591" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="9261" href="Poset.html#7416" class="Function">isDirected</a> <a id="9272" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9273" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="9277" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a><a id="9278" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9280" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9234" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="9282" href="Basis.html#1591" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="9284" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9286" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9227" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="9288" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9289" href="Frame.html#4300" class="Function Operator">⋁[</a> <a id="9292" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9294" href="Frame.html#4300" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="9296" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9234" class="Bound">U</a><a id="9297" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9299" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="9301" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9302" href="Frame.html#4300" class="Function Operator">⋁[</a> <a id="9305" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#634" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9307" href="Frame.html#4300" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="9309" href="Basis.html#5346" class="Function">⁅</a> <a id="9311" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9227" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="9313" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9317" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9315" href="Basis.html#5346" class="Function">∣</a> <a id="9317" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9317" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9319" href="Basis.html#5346" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="9321" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9234" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="9323" href="Basis.html#5346" class="Function">⁆</a><a id="9324" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Given a family `J` of Scott-continuous nuclei, everything in `J ^*` is
Scott-continuous.

Distributivity
--------------

<pre class="Agda"><a id="14605" class="Comment">{--
distr-N : [ isDist poset-of-nuclei _⊓N_ ⋁N_ ]
distr-N = {!!}

frame-of-nuclei-raw-str : RawFrameStr (ℓ-max ℓ₀ ℓ₁) ℓ₂ (Nucleus F)
frame-of-nuclei-raw-str = poset-of-nuclei-str , 𝟏 , _⊓N_ , ⋁N_

frame-of-nuclei-str : FrameStr (ℓ-max ℓ₀ ℓ₁) ℓ₂ (Nucleus F)
frame-of-nuclei-str = frame-of-nuclei-raw-str , axioms
  where
    axioms : [ FrameAx (poset-of-nuclei-str , 𝟏 , _⊓N_ , ⋁N_) ]
    axioms = 𝟏-top , (⊓N-meet , {!!} , {!!})

The final definition
--------------------

frame-of-nuclei : Frame (ℓ-max ℓ₀ ℓ₁) (ℓ-max ℓ₀ ℓ₁) ℓ₂
frame-of-nuclei =
  Nucleus F , frame-of-nuclei-raw-str , 𝟏-top , ⊓N-meet , {!!} , distr-N

-- --}</a>
<a id="15232" class="Comment">-- --}</a>
